I said... "For children this old, it's fine as long as someone is there to play with them. It should be doable. I think I can sum up Mr. Sheng's argument in two sentences. I don't know if I'm right. Those two sentences are... 'We welcome all who come, and we'll deliver it to the door of those who don't come.'"

"Children in the countryside, when they get a little older, have to tend cattle and chop firewood, so even if they want to come, they can't. And those little babies in arms can't be accepted even if they come. For these, we have no choice but to deliver education to their door. But for children like Qiaogu, three to five years old, we might as well open the door wide and say, 'We welcome all who come.' Because if they're not at home, there's less trouble at home. And if they enter school, the school won't be too burdened. I admit that Mr. Sheng has discovered a new continent today. But savoring Mr. Sheng's tone, it seems that the kindergartens in the city are not quite where they should be. I don't know if I'm guessing wrong?" Mr. Zhu said, "You're right! Let me tell you an interesting story. I heard this story indirectly, but it's absolutely true, not a joke. A young mistress loved to play mahjong more than anything else. She loved playing mahjong more than her child, who was a little angel, very cute. But spoiled from a young age, she inevitably threw tantrums sometimes. When this young mistress was engrossed in playing mahjong, her child would often come to bother her. One moment she wanted candy, the next she wanted wontons, one moment she was shouting to be scratched, the next she was shouting to pee, making the young mistress unable to settle down. She said to her child, 'If you keep bothering me like this, I'll send you to kindergarten.' The child didn't understand anything, and day by day she became a thorn in her mother's side. In the end, she hardened her heart and sent the child to kindergarten. Returning to the mahjong chair, she said with a grin, 'The little thing isn't here. Today I can play a few rounds to my heart's content.' Zhong'er! The teachers in the city's kindergartens have become the nannies of the young mistresses, helping them take care of their children so they can gamble without worry. Who will do the work of clearing the wilderness on these new continents?" I said, "Of course, we'll do it ourselves!"

Free Talk

Buying Firecrackers and Setting Them Off Yourself 141

My advocacy of democracy comes from practical experience. I believe that the purpose of politics is to seek the welfare of the people. To seek the welfare of the people, there must be a solidified relationship between the people and the land. The people and the land are born here and gather here; therefore, politics is nothing more than the words "birth" and "gathering." To enable the people to be born and to gather, they must be able to defend themselves and their land.

Why must the people protect themselves? Because only they know their own pain most thoroughly.

Why should the people defend their land? Because the land belongs to the people. Only when they own something do they know how to cherish it.

Why should local people manage local affairs? Because local people managing local affairs is like managing their own personal affairs. Managing one's own personal affairs is always done carefully and with a sense of responsibility; managing other people's affairs! You can be careless and not put in the effort.

I believe that the tools of politics are nothing more than two things: one is funding, and the other is talent, both of which must be drawn from the people. Since politics is for the people, it should be taken from the people and used for the people. However, it is not enough to just take from the people and use for the people; the people must take for themselves and use for themselves.

In conclusion, everyone is willing to buy firecrackers and set them off themselves; if you buy firecrackers and let someone else set them off, even a five-year-old will complain. This is the essence of democracy.

Anecdotes About Yu Hu 142

— Zheng Yimei

Old Yu's impeachment of Wang Zhengyou was a sound that shook the universe. A guest talked about his anecdotes, saying that Yu Youren and Hu Puan were both famous for their beautiful beards, so they were nicknamed Yu Hu. He used to be a news reporter and was also upright and outspoken. He once presided over the "Min Hu Bao" (People's Call) newspaper, advocating revolution. He was hated by the Qing court. A certain high official especially hated him to the bone, saying, "If I catch Yu, I will gouge out his eyes as punishment." Yu knew this and laughed it off, jokingly changing the "Min Hu Bao" (People's Call) to "Min Yu Bao" (People's Appeal). Removing the two dots from the character "呼" (hu, call) to make it "吁" (yu, appeal) is no different from a person having their eyes gouged out. His humor was like this. Old Yu was good at cooking mutton, having been taught by Mongolians. He had names like Genghis Khan Mutton and Caucasian Mutton, which were rich but not gamey, thick but not greasy, and were a special delicacy. The guest had once been full at Yu's house and praised it endlessly. Yu loved to eat pike lung. The pike is a fish with a swollen belly like a pufferfish, found in lakes and marshes. Its lungs are extremely tender. Cooking them into a soup is a fine delicacy. The Shi Family Restaurant in Xiangxi, Wu is especially good at making it. Old Yu would often quickly eat it when he was visiting Lingyan Temple. The character "魞" (pike) is not found in dictionaries, so he repeatedly examined and corrected it, and even wrote poems to promote it. On ordinary days, he wears green shoes and cloth socks, without a speck of dust. When he has time, he approaches the pond, his strength and unrestrainedness having an ancient charm. He also likes to write about recent works. I saw a vertical scroll he wrote at a friend's house, recording one of the miscellaneous poems of Hai Yu, which said: "Fallen leaves pile up silently, layer upon layer. In the empty mountain, the old man can still walk. I have idly traveled all the ancient temples in Jiangnan. I can also be counted as a wild monk from the West." Among politicians, Old Yu is worthy of the name of an elegant man without shame. He is truly admirable.

Record of Students and Volunteers Departing for the Northeast 143

— Yun Sun

Last year, when Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang were lost, more than 8,000 students and volunteers rose up in indignation in a corner of Songbin. By the time of the Shanghai Incident, fewer than 100 people ventured into the hail of bullets, disregarding their mortal bodies. I secretly think that there is a world of difference between sitting and talking and getting up and doing. Now, in addition to a part incorporated into the 19th Route Army Volunteers, I heard that only ten remained. These are the ten determined men who vowed not to change their minds, that is, the students and volunteers who the newspapers reported recently were about to depart for the Northeast. Yesterday, I met Mr. Zhang Wenzhong, a member of the regiment, who made the following remarks to the reporter. He said that since the puppet Manchukuo and the Japanese have already made a decision to recognize it, there is no other way to recover the lost land in the Northeast and rescue our compatriots in Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang other than by force. The Volunteer Army in the Northeast, numbering a million, lacks unified rule. If this continues, it is not the ultimate goal of long-term resistance. My comrades will go to the Northeast, without empty talk and high-sounding words, with the duty of uniting the volunteer army in the two provinces. My comrades have their own strengths and cooperate with each other, such as those who speak Japanese, who scout out the enemy's reality, and those who know the customs of the Northeast, who specialize in contacting all the patriots in the Northeast. Others who are proficient in both Chinese and English engage in internal and external propaganda work. They will complete their mission by meeting General Ma Zhanshan. As for the route out of the customs, they have also done their best in advance. If they go directly to Dalian, Vladivostok, etc., they will inevitably be spotted by the Japanese and their journey will be blocked. It has now been determined to go to Beiping first, turn to Rehe, and then exit Xifengkou. They are not afraid of the hardships of the mountains and rivers. They will break through the difficulties with a passionate heart.

I heard that the day the regiment's flag was headed north was this month. The 19th Route Army had a precedent telegram directly to Ma Zhanshan. Generals Cai Tingkai and Weng Zhaoyuan had personal letters of recommendation. When visiting Zhu Qinglan in Shanghai, they expressed their appreciation. When visiting Ma Zhanshan's representative, they also welcomed them sincerely. The gentlemen of the regiment were all students from the Middle School, Political Science, Zhengfeng College, Wen College, and Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School in this port. The authorities of each school praised the gentlemen for their patriotic indignation to save the country, kept their grades, and subsidized their travel expenses, in order to boost their morale. Zhang Wenzhong, who spoke with the reporter, had studied at Zhengfeng Wen College. When the Shanghai war broke out, he served as a war reporter for a news agency and also engaged in scouting. Miss Yao, of Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, is the niece of Yao Zirang, a famous person in Shanghai. She had taught in the Northeast. When she traveled to the Northeast, she served in the Volunteer Army twice, riding a horse and holding a gun, charging into battle. Mulan and Chonggu cannot be surpassed in front. Miss Yao returned to the south not long ago, and then vowed to abandon the pen and join the army, which is also magnificent.

A Record of the First Trial of Sound 144

— Tang Hao

The long-awaited sound and color film "A Laughing Fate" by Mingxing Company has recently been completed. The first episode was premiered at the Nanjing Grand Theater in this port on the morning of the previous day. At that time, the wind and rain were rushing in a fierce manner. The audience rushed to stop, their clothes and shoes were wet, but they did not think it was bitter. After the screening, they praised it endlessly.

On this day, the bell rang ten times. The music started and the silver light suddenly appeared. The main characters in the play, Ms. Hu Die, who plays both Shen Fengxi and He Lina, Xia Peizhen plays Guan Xiugu, Zheng Xiaoqiu plays Fan Jiashu, and Xiao Ying plays Guan Shoufeng, all act in a true and vivid manner, depicting the characters meticulously. For a time, people were intoxicated by the silver light, as if reliving old dreams and reuniting with old friends. The original impressions of Mr. Zhang Henshui's original work are very deep in everyone's minds. The performing art of this film has reached a perfect state.

The plot of the whole film starts with Jiashu wandering around Tianqiao and ends with Fengxi moving away. The story told is very plain. It is completely based on subtle expressions and genuine emotions. Among them, Jiashu and Shoufeng meet by chance, their hearts are touched by a word, and they quickly become intimate friends. Shoufeng is poor and sick, and a hero at the end of the road, his eyes are full of hot tears. When Fengxi hears Jiashu's words to abandon her studies, she is as if in a dream, and she can't help but cry with joy, and the shy, coquettish expression when she privately sends a photo, and the earnestness of her words when asking for a photo, etc., can always manipulate the audience's emotions of sorrow and joy unconsciously. This is a very valuable point. In addition, the lipstick mark left by Jiashu on the stage, the deep concealment of the curtains in Fengxi's boudoir, and Lina's repeated hints and efforts to show her love, are all extremely beautiful. This is a master of writing love.

The script is tightly and appropriately divided into scenes, interspersed with three different kinds of love, circling back and forth, and the descriptions are very elegant. It can be seen that Mr. Duhe has worked hard to cut and compile it. The words in the silent parts and the lines in the sound dialogues are all forceful and full of emotion. The excerpts are wonderful and unprecedented. The sound is very clear. The scenery is taken from many scenic spots in the old capital, and most of them are natural color films. The continuous projection on the white screen is bright and pleasing to the eye, no different from lying down and traveling. The overall performance of the play is excellent and can be called a masterpiece. It is said that the second episode will also be released soon, and it is expected to have new contributions.

A Stroll Along the Grand Canal (Part 1) 146

— Shanshan

(I) Farewell to West Lake

As the eastern sky just began to reveal a faint fish-belly white, I had already, together with the well-wishers—the second batch of patients who had not slept well that night—strolled swiftly past the desolate and mournful Tomb of Su Xiaoxiao, stepping onto the humorous yet slender Bai Causeway, heading towards the bustling corner of Hangzhou. The well-wishers advised me to take a car, but I strongly opposed it, because I wanted to take one last look at the scenery of the West Lake and mountains that I was about to leave behind. Although the night rain had stopped, the cotton-like damp clouds still heavily pressed on the tops of the mountains. The lake was shrouded in a light mist like silver gauze, and the lake water was still. At this time, there were no boats, nor could one hear the tinkling of shoe heels. I slowed my pace and quietly strode forward. Amidst the cries of "Poria Cake, Crystal Cake", I boarded the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau's bus bound for Nanjing. At just after six o'clock, I heard the last cry, a tragic and piercing call that seemed to determine my fate. At that moment, the bus had already started, and I simultaneously gave the last strand of my gaze to West Lake.

(II) Bamboo Path

The car had just passed the lakeside and turned a corner when it stopped outside a repair shop. Several workers began to repair the machinery. The passengers all stared at the workers' hands, their brows furrowed, seemingly impatient. I couldn't help but let out a sigh of helplessness. I thought to myself, "We Chinese people always embrace the Buddha's feet only at the last minute. The bus stops for repairs even as it is about to start."

Fortunately, the workers were quick. After only half an hour of repairs, the vehicle was able to drive smoothly again. The low pressure among the passengers also disappeared, and everyone looked very lively, especially their two flexible eyes.

The journey was smooth all the way. Before long, the vehicle drove onto the bamboo path between "Dong (Dong)" and "Shangbai (Shangbai)". This bamboo path, I am not exaggerating when I say, is at least six or seven li long. Both sides of the intoxicated red soil mountain road were densely lined with bamboo. The new green leaves were layered and piled up into a delicate green sea. Countless bamboo poles flickered with the speed of the car. These flickering, countless bamboo poles seemed like a flock of cranes dancing, or a hundred thousand ostriches racing.

(III) Miniature of the Three Gorges

The car galloped through the mountains, like an invincible beast walking on a familiar road every day, without hesitation or stagnation, sweeping across the red, eye-catching mountain trails like a gust of wind.

After passing Qingshan, the car climbed a hillside with great effort. At this time, steep cliffs stood on both sides of the road. These cliffs were so high that the sky was squeezed small. If the cliffs were a miniature of the mountains, and the car road was the vast Yangtze River, then isn't this a small model of the Three Gorges of Badong?

(IV) A Beautiful Painting

The passengers' eyes were all fixed on the window, without a word. Directly in front of me was a rectangular window. It was very interesting to look out from this rectangular window. Sometimes, one could see a corner of green hills peeking out from the pine forest. Sometimes, one could see a few figures moving on the red soil road sandwiched between the bright green of midsummer. The frame of this window was just like the frame of a painting. What was framed in the middle was the most beautiful corner of nature, a beautiful painting. But even if it is a beautiful painting, it can't change with the speed of the wheels like this landscape.

The Tale of the Horse Shuanglou (89)

— Master of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 11: An Official Parade in a Remote Town; A Group of Vulgar People Follow the Retinue

As they just entered the west gate of the county town, they had already alarmed the crowds in the city. Many men, women, old, and young gathered on both sides of the street, standing as if in a welcoming line, craning their necks to watch. It felt even more interesting than watching the City God go on parade. As they watched, the crowd even whispered to each other, exchanging private words. They corroborated their keen and accurate judgments. Those sitting in the two mule carts must be two high-ranking officials. They must be the big shots in this entourage. But there can't be two heads of equal status, so they guessed that it must be one civilian official and one military official, or one chief official and one deputy official. It was just a fleeting glimpse, and they couldn't clearly see the appearance of the two high-ranking officials. They couldn't rely on their smattering of knowledge of physiognomy to carefully assess who had better fortune and higher rank. They wanted to see how the future would turn out, like placing a bet, which was still a little regrettable. However, there was another place where they could confidently and accurately guess. They must be going to the Changxing Grand Hotel to rest their horses. This was what everyone believed, without any doubt. Because although there were many hotels in the city, there was really only one, the Changxing Grand Hotel, that was the best and largest in terms of layout and facilities. Traditionally, officials arriving from the provincial capital could not stoop to stay in small inns. Since the establishment of the Changxing Grand Hotel, it had monopolized all such official residences. This can be considered a common sense known to everyone in the area. There was no need for further discussion. Moreover, there was a special discovery in this entourage. The fat man at the very front, who looked like a judge riding a horse in a City God parade, was recognized by many as the most famous gentleman in the area. His official title and nickname were called Qiu Si Yanwang (Fourth Lord Qiu, the King of Hell), Qiu Jinlu, or Fourth Master Qiu. He always accompanied the county magistrate in and out of the county government, addressing the county magistrate as a brother, and sitting on an equal footing. He specialized in secretly arranging lawsuits for the elders of the village, fulfilling every request. Usually, if someone wanted to find him, there were only three places where they could find his traces. The first was the county government. The second was the small family he had established with a newlywed courtesan. The third was the Changxing Grand Hotel, where officials came and went. He had a room reserved there all year round, specifically for handling cases and discussing litigation, as if it were a law firm. Now, with his high status, he did not hesitate to lower himself to ride a horse for these two newly arrived high officials. It was conceivable that the status and influence of these two high officials were absolutely extraordinary.

Large Yarn Merchants Covered Short Positions, and the Yarn Market Reacted with an Upward Trend 152

The Cotton Yarn Market Initially Fell and Then Rose, With an Unusually Chaotic Situation. The Continued Decline in Prices Led to Large Merchants Covering Short Positions, Resulting in a Sudden Reaction and Rise. This Kind of Situation Is a Common Phenomenon. Moreover, the Price Has Fallen by 16 or 17 Taels From the Peak. It Would Not Be Surprising If It Returned to 3, 5, or 2 Taels. However, in Reality, There Is Still Not Much Optimism. Due to the Weakness of Rural Areas, Economic Bankruptcy, and the Weak Purchasing Power of Various Parties, Coupled with the Fierce Competition From Japanese Merchants, the Future Depends on Actual Facts as the Biggest Key.

Cotton Market Quiet Situation 153

The cotton market remains calm, but the buying interest is strong. Due to rising gold prices, sentiment is firm, and buyers are eager to increase their positions. However, factory demand is stagnant as factories already have enough foreign cotton. There is no capacity for domestic cotton. It is said that 400,000 to 600,000 bales of American cotton may be sold to our country on credit, and both parties have reached a compromise on the terms and procedures. If this becomes a reality, it will have a significant impact on domestic cotton. Therefore, in the afternoon, Sincere and major players dumped large quantities. However, general retail cotton merchants were buying, holding onto their holdings, due to rising margins. In short, given the overall situation, it is difficult to predict the future.

Zheng Standard Fluctuations are Minimal. The Zheng Standard market opened with American cotton weak, and there were few buyers in the market. Prices fell by 1.5 cash for each month. The afternoon opening was very weak, and major players were selling, softening the market. The closing price rose by 1.2 cash due to the better gold market. The total trading volume for the day was 53,500 dan. Sales included Changfeng 3,500 dan, Sincere 5,200 dan, and Changhe 2,000 dan. Purchases included Suilong 1,500 dan, Rongxing 1,400 dan, Renfeng 1,500 dan, and Gengfeng 1,200 dan. The closing prices are listed below:

Northeast Customs Seized Meilehe's Remarks 164

Fukumoto Violates Laws

Has Been Dismissed by the Ministry of Finance

Reuters Shanghai News, Chinese Customs Commissioner Meilehe, yesterday issued the following remarks on the Northeast Customs issue: "Manchukuo" authorities, originally the restrictions imposed on the remittance of tax funds to Shanghai, and the recent robbery of this revenue, have been used to pay off indemnities and foreign debts guaranteed by customs duties, greatly diminishing. Now that all kinds of commerce are seeing depression, resulting in shrinking tax revenue, the Northeast Customs problem, if prolonged, will greatly affect the obligation to repay indemnities and foreign debts, and domestic debts dependent on customs revenue will also face the same danger. The financial situation has been further worsened by the extraordinary actions of Fukumoto, the Dalian Customs Commissioner. Fukumoto, a Japanese, refused to comply with the instructions of the Chief Customs Commissioner, not allowing the banks in Dalian to remit the local tax funds to Shanghai, on the grounds that he had received a letter from Kawai, the Director of the Diplomatic Department of the Kwantung Government, stating that under the current circumstances, remitting tax funds to Shanghai would be a highly provocative action. If remitted, the "Manchukuo" authorities would implement countermeasures and greatly harm the interests of the Japanese in the Kwantung Leased Territory. Therefore, he (Kawai) strongly advocated that the remittance should be postponed until the current dispute is resolved. The Chief Customs Commissioner, upon receiving this strange news, telegraphed the Customs Commissioner, objecting to his passive attitude, and ordered him to remit immediately. If he did not comply with the instructions, it would be regarded as insubordination. The Customs Commissioner subsequently telegraphed the following reply: "The passive attitude is the only one possible for me at present. I am consciously warned by the responsible Japanese authorities that if the Dalian Customs openly breaks with the 'Manchukuo' authorities, it will destroy the interests of the Japanese. As a Japanese, I cannot be tolerated if I promote such a break, and it violates my conscience. I implore the Chief Customs Commissioner to understand my difficulty in not being able to bear the responsibility." Now, because Fukumoto disobeyed the orders, he has been dismissed by the Minister of Finance, Song Ziwen. Fukumoto's violation of legal orders is unprecedented in the history of Chinese Customs.

Three Groups Issue Foreign Declaration on Northeast Customs 165

Please Urge Friendly Countries to Take Measures to Stop It

Reuters Shanghai News, the Shanghai Banking Association, the Qianye Association, and the National Federation of Commerce Associations, yesterday issued a foreign declaration on the Northeast Customs issue. The translation is as follows: Japan, through its own puppet state, seizes Northeast Customs. This move not only violates existing treaties, but also threatens the collapse of Chinese finance and politics. Northeast tax revenue accounts for 15% of the national customs revenue. China's important domestic and foreign debts are guaranteed by customs duties. If China's tax revenue is so seriously exploited, it will lead to extremely unfortunate consequences, plunging China into a long period of political and financial chaos. In order to safeguard the dignity of the treaty and to safeguard international trade and financial relations, friendly countries should take measures to stop Japan from implementing this tactic in order to avoid the collapse of China. Delay may be too late to save.

Hope that the Advanced Figures of the Party and the State

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, being very concerned about the Nanjing special telegram published in various newspapers in this port yesterday, concerning the remarks of Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, on the opium policy, issued the following statement by its spokesperson yesterday afternoon. Yesterday's newspaper reported that President Wang said that in recent years, opium has not been banned in various parts of our country, and has become an open secret. At a time when the country's finances are extremely exhausted, it is better to implement openness, prohibiting it in the levy and implementing the ban on one side and gaining a source of wealth on the other to relieve the current financial difficulties. There are many people who make this proposal, but the central government has not yet made a decision because of the importance of the relationship. If there are other remedial measures, it is absolutely unwilling to implement this final policy. However, if it is handled properly, such as the policy of prohibiting it in the levy in India and the Philippines, the effect is not as bad as generally imagined. Wang's remarks followed closely after the central government reiterated the opium ban, which is tantamount to exposing the contradictions in the government's policy and expressing no sincerity or determination to ban smoking. The investigation of opium is not forbidden, not impossible to ban, but the government is unwilling to ban it. Otherwise, it can be banned at the end of the Qing Dynasty, and Hu cannot be banned today. Han Fuju in Shandong can be banned, and the central government Hu cannot be banned. If it is considered impossible to ban it because it is not banned, it is self-deception. If there is a desire not to ban it, so that the smoking disaster spreads, and then used as a reason for open sale, is it not a plan to cover one's ears and steal the bell? Wang also said, "It is better to implement openness, prohibiting it in the levy and implementing the ban on one side." If one side relies on opium as a source of wealth and the other side implements a ban, such a contradictory and contradictory approach, even a child knows that there is no such reason. If you want to collect taxes, you can't ban it. If you want to ban it, you should sacrifice the tobacco tax. In short, those who prohibit it in the levy actually levy it without banning it. If you want to ban smoking, you should take the method of banning it without levying it. It is also said that "If there are other remedial measures, it is absolutely unwilling to implement this final policy." The government has the natural duty to protect the people, this is an easy definition, even if there is no way to think of it, it should not implement a policy that harms the people. If the skin is gone, what will the hair be attached to? Premier Sun Yat-sen's legacy of rejecting drugs said, "The declaration of war on opium must never be compromised. If a responsible government agency, for its own private convenience, lowers the flag and stops the war on opium, no matter how long, it is an act of treason." If this so-called final opium public sale method is implemented, where is the legacy of Premier Sun Yat-sen? Today, the authorities who claim to be loyal followers of Premier Sun Yat-sen will not act for their own private convenience. It is also said that "The United Kingdom in India, the United States in the Philippines, have adopted a policy of prohibiting it in the levy, and its effect is not as bad as generally imagined." The Indians have suffered deeply from opium, which is one of the reasons for the demise of the country. The Indians have been groaning and seeking liberation during the British rule in India. Gandhi's anti-British thought arose from dissatisfaction with the British opium policy in India. Even the British opposed the government's policy. How can our government follow it to slaughter its own compatriots? As for the Philippines, it has adopted a complete ban policy. The US government has not collected a cent of tobacco tax. If the government adopts this policy, we would welcome it very much. As for the policy of prohibiting it in the levy, how is the performance? The party and the country are very fortunate.

Japanese Riverboats Under Navy Management 167

Implemented from Yesterday

Since the withdrawal of Japanese troops from Shanghai, the tasks of protecting overseas Chinese in Shanghai are all the responsibility of the Navy. Recently, ships and troops have been added along the Yangtze River, and no effort has been spared. Renting ships for military use, managing merchant ships, and assisting in the transportation of Japanese goods in order to break our country's rejection of goods. Recently, inferior goods have been imported very crowded, and more are imported into the Yangtze River. The actions of the Japanese Navy will be investigated and recorded as follows:

Management of Riverboats. The shipping of Nisshin Co. is the largest in the Yangtze River, with more than 20 ships, operating in the upper and lower reaches of each port. After the January 28th Incident, all business was suspended, and the Japanese Navy rented the Daifuku No. 94 ship, running from Shanghai to Wuhan, for the transportation of materials and the like. After the withdrawal of troops, the leased ships were returned to Nisshin on June 1. However, because the Chinese refused to transport Japanese ships after the war, Nisshin's Yangtze River ships had no way to resume business. Unexpectedly, the Japanese Navy in Shanghai contacted Nisshin again and continued to rent several first-class riverboats of the company, such as the Fengyang Maru, Nanyang Maru, and Xiangyang Maru, from yesterday, still running from Shanghai to Wuhan. All operations are under the management of the Navy. On the upper river side, there is also the Xinyang Maru, running from Wuhan to Yichang, also under the management of the Navy. Chinese buyers do not get on the ship, because the management is under the Navy.

Escorting Japanese Goods. Japanese goods have recently been imported very crowded. Nisshin Post's special Sino-Japanese liners to Shanghai are always full of loads, most of which are transported to the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River. Since Chinese ships do not transport them on behalf, they are all transferred by Japanese ships. Using the Navy to transport rented ships, packing Japanese goods to the Yangtze River, on the surface, can be listed as military supplies, transported out of Wusong to hide the eyes and ears of the Chinese people, and landing at the port is more convenient. The company can also deny it, one stroke and several good preparations, its intention is deep, the plan is周, it is not国人所能察知, so the Japanese goods运数千吨.

Japanese Warships Withdraw. The Japanese Navy fleet in Shanghai has completely withdrawn, leaving only four torpedoes from the 15th Squadron, because they巡长江, 末归国也. The current warships have been电令归国 by the Japanese Navy. Three torpedo ships of the team have already奉令载海軍 three teams. They left Shanghai yesterday morning and returned to Sasebo directly. The Japanese warships left in Shanghai are now only gunboats and torpedo boats.

Flagship is Coming Soon. Shanghai Japanese Navy has been列入 First Outside遣队内所辖, from沪至汉, Shang达宜昌, originally派日舰 fourteen艘者,今已扩至 twenty艘矣, a 遣队司令驻沪, 惟近日日海軍为增厚驻华海軍实力计, specially将第三艦隊司令旗艦出云,移驻沪上, the new commander, Zuo 近司, reported to Shanghai yesterday by电沪, that he has乘出云舰, from Sasebo to Shanghai today, at the latest on the 28th, he can抵申, after that, the Japanese warships in the Yangtze River are all under his command, and the third team of warships is temporarily stationed in Japan, which can also be transferred to Shanghai when necessary, there was no such commander before the January 28th Incident, it was only added after the war.

Extraterritorial Road Construction Pending Case 168

Continued Negotiations Yesterday

Principles Are No Longer Different

The Two Sides Temporarily Keep Secret

The pending case of the extraterritorial road construction by the Shanghai Public Concession Bureau has been brought to a conclusion after negotiations between the representatives of the Public Concession Bureau and the representatives of the Municipal Government. After approval by the authorities of both sides, it can be finally resolved. The Board of Directors of the Public Concession Bureau had once discussed the case last Wednesday. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also recently approved and sent it to Shanghai. There is no longer any objection to the agreed principle. However, a few points need to be revised in the articles. Municipal Government Representative Yu Hongjun and Public Concession Bureau Representative Fei Ren Xindun continued to meet at 12:30 yesterday afternoon to discuss the points that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs indicated needed to be revised. They dispersed in about an hour. The negotiation process was very harmonious. Both sides now hope to continue to meet within the next week. After about two more meetings, the case can be resolved satisfactorily.

Yu Hongjun Speaks. A reporter from the East China News Agency visited Secretary-General Yu at the Municipal Government yesterday afternoon and asked about the content of the negotiations. According to Yu, both parties are eager to resolve this negotiation as soon as possible, so although there are many difficulties in the negotiations, they can still understand each other. The points that we have revised are difficult to publish temporarily because we respect the intentions of both parties, but the principle has not changed. There are many modifications in the wording, and so is the other party. According to the current situation, it can be completely resolved after one more meeting. However, before signing, I will decide to publicly solicit opinions from all walks of life to show that there is no loss of sovereignty. My negotiation will be based on the principle of not giving up sovereignty. The reason for the temporary secrecy is that once it is publicly announced, it will cause misunderstandings and hinder the progress of the matter. Although this negotiation is a local event, the Municipal Government will solicit the opinions of the Central Government at any time. The opposition of the expatriates of various countries is expected. There is no reason at first, and there is no need to refute it.

Fei Xindun Speaks. The reporter visited Mr. Fei Xindun, the Director of the Public Concession Bureau, yesterday and asked whether the Public Concession Bureau has full power to resolve the case, or whether it needs to be approved by the Consular Corps. Fei replied that this case is currently being resolved by the Public Concession Bureau, and there is no need to ask the Consular Corps for instructions.

The content is temporarily not published. As for the agreed content, both representatives will not publish it for the time being because it is not the time yet. However, it is roughly the same as what our newspaper previously published. The outline is that the extraterritorial road construction area is divided into a special administrative region, and the Municipal Government and the Public Concession Bureau each recommend half of the personnel to form an administrative committee. The chairman is appointed by the Municipal Government, and the vice-chairman is recommended by the Public Concession Bureau. A special police force is formed to maintain law and order. The patrol chief is appointed by the Municipal Government, and the vice-patrol chief is recommended by the Public Concession Bureau. The administrative expenses are borne jointly by the Municipal Government and the Public Concession Bureau. The patrol tax and health affairs are all under the Public Concession Bureau. The Municipal Public Utility Bureau can issue special licenses for electricity, telephone, and tap water, and the three companies of the concession can undertake it.

HUPU ARSENAL STILL HAS HOPE FOR CONTINUATION 169

LIN AND WANG, TWO REPRESENTATIVES, RETURNED YESTERDAY TO REPORT

CHEN YI HAS ORDERED THE HANDLING COMMITTEE TO TEMPORARILY POSTPONE PROCEEDINGS

According to the Guowen News Agency, the Shanghai Arsenal was almost shut down due to a report submitted by two Western advisors to the Ordnance Department, Bruce and Martin. Before that, the arsenal sent three representatives to the capital: Hu Sihong, Chief of the Review Department; Lin Weirong, Director of the Bullet Factory; and Wang Cheng, Director of the Shell Factory. They explained the situation to the Ministry of Military Affairs. Now, Directors Lin and Wang have returned to Shanghai yesterday morning to report to their colleagues at the arsenal on the negotiations in the capital. However, Hu Sihong is still staying in the capital. The following is a record of yesterday's situation and interviews with Lin and Wang:

Three Factories to Be Shut Down This time, the arsenal shutdown does not only include the Shanghai Arsenal, but also the Jinan Arsenal in Shandong Province and the Huayin Arsenal in Shaanxi Province. The plan was to merge the equipment of these three factories into the Jinling, Hanyang, and Gongxian Arsenals. Subsequently, both the Jinan and Huayin Arsenals explained the advantages and disadvantages to the government, and were thus preserved. Moreover, the Huayin Arsenal is currently under construction, and it would be particularly difficult to order a shutdown at this time. However, according to news obtained by reporters from other sources regarding the Shanghai Arsenal, the results of Hu, Lin, and Wang's trip to Beijing to explain the situation is that the Ministry must seek instructions from the Military Affairs Commission regarding whether to shut down the arsenal or not. As Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has not yet sent a reply, it is still unknown. However, the first step achieved by the three representatives is that if they had not gone to Beijing, the Jinling, Hanyang, and Gongxian Arsenals would have already sent personnel to Nanjing and then to Hangzhou, planning to allocate and collect the equipment from the Shanghai Arsenal that was to be sent to Hangzhou. Now, not only are the collection personnel staying in the capital, but the organization of the handling committee has also been instructed by Acting Minister Chen Yi to temporarily postpone proceedings. Therefore, the Shanghai Arsenal still has a glimmer of hope for not being shut down, and everything must await Chiang Kai-shek's reply.

The Shanghai Arsenal's Assets The reporter believes that it seems too uneconomical to abandon the original factory buildings of the Shanghai Arsenal and allocate them to the three Jinling arsenals, and then build new buildings. However, according to someone familiar with the arsenal's affairs, the situation is not entirely like this. The arsenal only has land in Shanghai, nearly 800 mu, and the Pudong ammunition depot has 40 to 50 mu. Moreover, establishing a commercial factory along the Huangpu River is quite suitable. Calculating at 4,000 yuan per mu, this income will exceed 4.5 million yuan. With this, what worries are there about building new factory buildings? Therefore, the central government abolished the Shanghai Arsenal and allocated it to the three arsenals in Jinling and other places, actually because of this. Otherwise, at a time when finances are exhausted, increasing this construction cost would probably not be possible, let alone having factory buildings that can be sold. The reporter believes that what they said is reasonable, so I will record it.

Interview with the Two Representatives Yesterday, the reporter heard that Lin Weirong, Director of the Bullet Factory, and Wang Cheng, Director of the Shell Factory, who went to Beijing, had returned to Shanghai during the agricultural break. The reporter immediately rushed to inquire about the process. According to the two representatives, Lin and Wang, we arrived in Beijing on the 21st and, together with Director Hu and Chen Shihong, Director of the Cannon Factory, who was staying in Beijing for official business, we paid a visit to Chen Yi, Acting Minister of Military Affairs, and explained in detail: (1) The dismantling and transportation of the Shanghai Arsenal's machines to Hangzhou will take more than four months. If methods are not devised to install them as soon as possible, they may rust and become unusable. (2) When dismantling the machines, due to the emergency situation, the parts of one machine were packed into several boxes, or the parts of several machines were packed into one box. Therefore, if the Shanghai Arsenal's machines are moved and installed as a whole, there will be no difficulty. If the suggestions of the German advisors Bruce and Martin, who are unfamiliar with the situation of the Shanghai Arsenal, are adopted, and the Shanghai Arsenal's machines are distributed to the three Jinling, Hanyang, and Gongxian Arsenals, it is feared that due to the chaotic parts, most of the machines will be discarded. (3) If the machines are distributed to various factories, each factory must also build factory buildings and increase power, which is actually a waste of resources. It is better to preserve the entire factory and use the old site, or move to another site to build a house and use commercial electricity, which is cheaper. (4) The Shanghai Arsenal has produced excellent products at low cost over the years. During the Ordnance Department's performance appraisal, it was ranked first. During this anti-Japanese war, all the workers of the arsenal worked hard together under dangerous circumstances, risking their lives. The output of ammunition to support the 19th Route Army in one month was almost equal to the output of the past two and a half months. The Ordnance Department once issued an order to commend and comfort them beyond the ordinary. Later, they were ordered to dismantle the machines and move them to Zhejiang Province, originally hoping to determine the factory base as soon as possible and start work as soon as possible. However, for four months, there has been no news. Some of the employees who have been suspended with pay and the temporary dismissed workers have hanged themselves or drowned themselves due to economic pressure. The weak are like this, and the strong will take risks. Therefore, Vice Minister Chen was very clear about the reasons why the machines should be installed as soon as possible and should not be dispersed, and he was very concerned about maintaining the entire Shanghai Arsenal so that workers would not lose their jobs, so as to emphasize the national economy. He promised to forward a telegram to Chairman Chiang, asking him to reconsider the suggestions of the German advisors, hoping that the future progress of the Shanghai Arsenal would be in line with the principles of developing the national economy and people's livelihood. Later, Lin and Wang also said that after visiting Vice Minister Chen, they also visited Hong Zhong, Director of the Ordnance Department, and visited the heads of various departments in the department, explaining the situation of the Shanghai Arsenal in detail based on the facts. Previously, the Ordnance Department had an "Equipment and Materials Handling Committee for the Shanghai Arsenal" organized based on the suggestions of the German advisors. Now, Chen instructed that before Nanjing receives Chairman Chiang's reply, the committee plans to postpone the proceedings. In short, whether the Shanghai Arsenal will be shut down has not yet been officially ordered, and there is no phenomenon of rushing to complete the factory. Now, this proposal to preserve the entire Shanghai Arsenal's machines and not disperse them to various factories to cause losses has been accepted by Chen, so the Shanghai Arsenal should not be destroyed. It is heard that Lin and Wang will still need to go to Beijing in the next few days to complete the work with Hu Sihong.

ANTI-EPIDEMIC VOICE CAUSES A LABOR STRIKE IN THE CHINESE PHARMACEUTICAL INDUSTRY 170

THE REASON IS A MATTER OF LABOR-MANAGEMENT CONDITIONS

REFUSAL OF OUTSIDE WORKERS AS SUBSTITUTES LEADS TO STRIKE

All the employees of the Chinese Medicine Industry in this city held a membership meeting yesterday because the capitalists ordered outside workers to join the trade union, and disputes occurred at that time. Fortunately, the police officers of the Public Security Bureau stopped them, and many important cases were resolved. The details of each situation are recorded below:

Cause of the Labor Strike The Pharmaceutical Industry Association, the outside workers and inside workers, have been divided by the Central Training Department of the Ministry of Industry. Regarding the issue of outside workers as substitutes, it was resolved at a meeting on June 15 that outside shop assistants should be registered and introduced by the association to each store to fill in as substitutes, and that the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union should be rejected from sending outside workers as substitutes. It was stipulated that members who violated the regulations would be expelled from membership and notified to each store to comply. This led to disputes in pharmacies such as Feng Cunren and Cai Tongde refusing to send substitute workers from the union. On the 23rd, more than 5,000 employees were summoned by the union to a meeting of representatives of workers from various districts. Because the matter was of great importance, a membership meeting was held to discuss the direction of the work.

Workers' Congress Yesterday at 2 p.m., pharmaceutical workers held a congress of members' representatives at the Yaowang Temple in Xiaonanmen. Members of the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau were sent to guide the meeting. More than 1,200 members' representatives were present. Zhao Zhenhui, Yuan Pinzhang, Feng Jikang, Cai Shenxiu, Chen Yuantao, and other five people were the presidium. First, Zhao Zhenhui reported that the capitalists have repeatedly unreasonably suppressed, disregarded the overall situation, and the suffering of unemployed workers, which is hateful. Then, the chairmen reported on the work one after another and began to discuss it.

Dispute Occurs During the discussion, regarding the capitalists' refusal to allow outside workers as substitutes, some workers advocated a general strike to promote the capitalists' awareness. Representatives of the Party and government organs tried their best to dissuade them. Later, Fang Zheng, who had been expelled from the union, made a speech without permission, which led to a dispute. The situation was very serious, and the order in the whole field was chaotic. Fortunately, the police officers from the Third Branch of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau were dispatched to maintain order, which calmed the situation and continued the discussion.

Resolution of Important Cases The general assembly resolved the following items: (1) How to deal with the capitalists' pharmaceutical industry association breaking the conditions? Resolution: (A) Unanimously opposed, (B) Issue a declaration to refute the association, (C) Warn the capitalists; (2) How to deal with the capitalists using differentiation methods to refuse substitute workers? Resolution: (A) Petition to higher authorities for assistance, (B) If a certain store refuses outside substitute workers, the outside workers of that store will be ordered to strike, (C) If a certain store's strike fails to achieve victory, then everyone will rise up to help; (3) How to deal with the association's enticement of outside workers to join? Resolution: Outside workers unanimously and automatically oppose; (4) Request higher authorities to restore the name of the workers' union. Resolution: Passed; (5) Request the capitalists to increase wages by 10 yuan per month for each person. Resolution: Passed; (6) Unemployed members of this association request the capitalists to arrange for them to be employed. Resolution: Must be controlled by this association; (7) Lower-level organization of this association. Resolution: The district branches should be responsible for stepping up organization; (8) The term of office of the directors and supervisors of this association has expired. Should they be re-elected on a regular basis? Resolution: Postpone the re-election; (9) How to deal with Cai Tongde not sending representatives to attend? Resolution: Send a letter to warn them, and those previously arranged by this association to employ workers will be driven out and replaced with other unemployed members; (10) Should a committee to demand wage increases be established? Resolution: Organize a wage increase movement committee, and elect Xie Shifang, Fang Qingjian, Zhang Tongfu, Yuan Pinzhang, Feng Jikang, Chen Yuantao, Zhao Zhenhui, Fang Qinghe, Zhu Jiaqing, Han Bingshou, Yang Xihui, Cai Shenxiu, Hu Hanrong, Shi Zongliang, Ma Weixin, and other 15 people as members; (11) How to deal with Cai Tongde in the concession if their ability is not achieved? Resolution: Petition to the higher authorities to transfer the patrol protection; (12) Should the unemployed members of this association be organized? Resolution: The organization section is responsible for organizing the unemployed group.

THE NAVY'S JIANGFENG AIRCRAFT IS SAFE 171

IT LANDED IN HAIYAN DUE TO BAD WEATHER

THREE OF THE FOUR AIRCRAFT RETURNED MIDWAY

JIANGFENG ARRIVED AT GAO CHANG MIAO YESTERDAY AFTERNOON FOR REPAIRS

The Jiangfeng aircraft of the Naval Aircraft Office in Gaochangmiao of this port, which departed from Hangzhou the day before yesterday, along with Jiangpeng, Jiangyan, and Jianghong, to come to Shanghai, had changing weather when it flew to Haiyan. Jiangfeng had no choice but to land, and the others also returned to Hangzhou due to headwinds. Yesterday morning, Jiangfeng continued to fly to Shanghai, and the people and the plane were safe. The following is a record of the process:

Aircraft Move to Hangzhou Since Shen Dexie took office as the factory director of the Naval Aircraft Office, a part of the aircraft was moved to the Hongqiao Airport for the use of training students to drive. Only three or four seaplanes were placed in Shangchangmiao. Later, due to the Japanese army's operations in Shanghai, fearing that they would be destroyed, they were all moved to Jianqiao, Hangzhou. However, the aircraft arrived soon after and two aircraft were bombed. The remaining aircraft were moved to West Lake, including Jianghong, Jiangou, Jiangpeng, Jiangyan, Jiangyi, Jiangyang, Jiangyuan, Jiangkun, Jiangfeng, and other nine reconnaissance aircraft. Now that Shen believes that the Shanghai war has been settled, he ordered them to fly back to Shanghai one after another.

Four Aircraft Departed Director Shen of the office ordered them to fly to Shanghai. Except for Jiangou, which returned to Shanghai earlier, Jiangfeng, Jianghong, Jiangyan, and Jiangpeng also flew to Shanghai the day before yesterday. The weather was very good when they departed from Hangzhou on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. It was very good. Unexpectedly, the weather suddenly changed near Haiyan. The original plan was to travel 280 li per hour, but due to headwinds, it was only 100 li. It was expected that it would take one and a half hours to reach Shanghai. After flying about 200 li, it had not yet reached Huangpu. Therefore, the three Jianghong aircraft feared that there would not be enough fuel and returned midway, but at that time only the Jiangfeng aircraft still bravely moved forward.

Forced to Land The driver of Jiangfeng was the Westerner Puri, who was the instructor of the office. When he flew near Haiyan, he already felt the headwind. Soon he did not see the three aircraft behind him, and the weather in Haiyan was even worse. Therefore, he had to land on the inland river. It was already 4 p.m. at that time. After Puri inspected the entire aircraft, he was unable to fly to Shanghai, so he stayed overnight on the river.

Jiangfeng Arrives in Shanghai Jiangfeng was not damaged. It continued to fly the next morning and flew away from Haiyan at 7:20 a.m. and arrived in Shanghai at 8:45 a.m. Because it was a seaplane, it landed in the Huangpu River in front of the Naval Aircraft Office in Gaochangmiao. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency arrived at the factory at noon and saw that Jiangfeng had entered the factory and was being inspected. As for the three aircraft that returned to Hangzhou, it is said that the weather is good today and they will still fly to Shanghai.

OVERSEAS CHINESE RETURNING FROM JAPAN YESTERDAY 173

A Total of More Than 100 People

The Navigation Bureau Sent Personnel to Take Care of Them

The poor overseas Chinese living in Japan, who are engaged in occupations such as hairdressing and tailoring, have very difficult lives. Since the deterioration of Sino-Japanese relations and the outbreak of the Shanghai war, they have been particularly excluded by the Japanese. The number of unemployed people is numerous. Our country's consulate in Japan convened and registered them, and telegraphed to foreign ports. The government ordered the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau to negotiate with the local Dala Company. The company's merchant ships transported them back to the country in batches. The first batch of more than 100 people arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the Wilson ship of Dala Company. The ship was berthed at the Bailianjing Wharf in Pudong. The Navigation Administration Bureau also sent personnel to take care of them. A small steamer transferred them to land. Most of the overseas Chinese went to live with their relatives and friends. Only a few people were sent by the Navigation Administration Bureau to charitable organizations to stay temporarily and provide food.

GANSHANG TELEGRAM ASKING FOR THE REPEAL OF THE PRODUCTION AND SALES TAX 179

The Jiangxi Business Gang of the Shanghai Business Gang Association received news from Gansheng yesterday that the production and sales tax was being levied. It immediately invited various guest gangs to a meeting to decide to telegram the Executive Yuan of the National Government, the Ministry of Finance and Industry, and the Jiangxi Provincial Government to repeal it immediately. The original telegram is as follows: "Your Excellency Wang, President of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, I recently learned that the Jiangxi Provincial Government decided to levy a production and sales tax on goods and set up checkpoints along the way, which is no different from the revival of Lijin. We were very surprised to hear the news. Gansheng has suffered from natural disasters and bandits in recent years, and the people have nothing left to eat. Now, we have received news of this exorbitant levy. After the robbery, how can the merchants and people bear this? I beg you to quickly order the Jiangxi Provincial Government to repeal the production and sales tax regulations and abide by the national prestige of cutting Lijin and relieving the people of Gansheng. We are anxiously awaiting your orders." The Shanghai Business Gang Association and the Jiangxi Business Gang bowed respectfully.

SHACHANG ALLIANCE ASKS FOR THE REPEAL OF THE SPECIAL COTTON TAX 180

The Chinese Cotton Mill Association had previously telegraphed the central government, requesting that the special business tax implemented by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, including cotton, be rectified and recorded. Some time ago, the association received a batch of instructions from the Ministry of Finance, stating that the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance had been ordered to abolish the clause. However, in recent days, it has been heard that the tax will be levied on July 1. Therefore, the association yesterday telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance again, strictly ordering the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to stop the special business tax. The financial ministry's instructions and the association's telegram are recorded separately below:

Instructions from the Ministry of Finance: "I have received your letter. I have checked the case of the Jiangsu Provincial Government's handling of the special business production and sales tax. I have already presented it to the Executive Yuan for instructions to open, and I will order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to still follow the previous order to abolish the tax. The Ministry has again ordered the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to abolish it in accordance with the original plan of the Executive Yuan, and will also send a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation to inform them." This is the batch.

Re-telegram Appeal: "Your Excellencies Wang, President of the Executive Yuan of the Nanjing National Government, and Song, Minister of Finance, I previously telegraphed the Ministry and Province, requesting that the special business tax implemented by Su Province be stopped, as it is a disguised form of Lijin and violates the central government's Lijin cutting order, and especially goes against the principle of a single tax on a single item. I also heard that the government strictly ordered it to be stopped, and the people were delighted. It is true that I am grateful, but roads are being promoted, and the Su Provincial Government is disregarding everything and still setting the tax to be levied on July 1. I was shocked to hear that the laws are being ignored and the merchants are being harmed. From the perspective of the textile industry, the association is taking the cotton levy of the special business tax. The disadvantages are already innumerable. I am here to tell you that I have checked the abolition of Lijin last year and changed to a unified tax, which is based on the principle of a single tax on a single item. I swore to the world that the burden on merchants and people has increased several times more than in the past, but the merchants are happy and have no complaints. The original intention was to add tax revenue to the country and relieve the pain of Lijin. Unexpectedly, after more than a year, the Lijin of disguised forms has been revived, and the credibility of the central government has been swept away. This is one of the things that cannot be done. I have also checked that the textile factories in Su Province are concentrated in Shanghai. The factories set up in the interior are in the minority. They used to use local products and local sales, and they can barely gain a foothold. In recent years, cotton production has been poor, and most of the raw cotton is imported from abroad. The people in the interior are poor, and their purchasing power has decreased sharply. The cooked goods must be sold abroad, and transportation costs are increased. Compared with Shanghai factories, it is difficult to survive. If all the factories within the scope of Su Province are levied a special cotton business tax, according to the province's announcement, the American cotton tax is 1.28 yuan per stone, which is 4.48 yuan per package of cotton yarn. The factories that are not under the jurisdiction of Su Province have nothing to do with it. Such a malformed burden, in law and in sentiment, is not based on the machine. If the country is related to financial resources and restores the national Lijin, there is no room for merchants to complain. If it is implemented alone in a corner of Su Province, even Shanghai is excluded. This is what the Su Province textile industry is determined to oppose and cannot recognize. This is the second thing that cannot be done. The great disease of Lijin lies in setting up checkpoints to collect taxes, making things difficult, and the officials are also extorting money, harming the country and the merchants like snakes and scorpions. If you have a little common sense, you can say it. If you don't have a different mind, how can you bear to say it again? This is the third thing that cannot be done. Based on the above, in order to respect national laws, to consider the hardships of merchants, and to avoid disadvantages, the special business tax that Su Province intends to implement must not be allowed to be governed by the province and freely implemented. Moreover, Su Province is close to the capital, and the orders are still not being followed. No wonder foreigners place me as an unorganized country. If Su Province is in financial difficulties and there is no way to take measures, it should also be done separately. The method of opening up should not be the policy of depleting the lake. The merchants and people are painfully stripped of their skin and are eager to choose. For the sake of repeated appeal, I respectfully ask the chief to examine and approve the strict order for the Jiangsu Provincial Government's special business tax to be stopped immediately, so as to pay attention to the achievements and to care about the merchants. I am extremely grateful and awaiting orders." The Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Association respectfully bowed.

SCOUTS DEPART FOR THE WAR ZONE 182

TO TAKE ON EPIDEMIC PREVENTION AND DISINFECTION WORK

The Shanghai War Zone Relief Committee, in view of the inevitability of epidemics after the great war, and the fact that cholera has been discovered in early summer, has organized a war zone epidemic prevention and disinfection team to eliminate and prevent the spread of epidemics. The locations are divided into four districts: Baoshan, Jiading, Taicang, and Kunshan. The Committee has requested the Er Tang Scout Group of the China Scout 270th Group and the 65th Commercial and Industrial Scout Group of this city to take on this work. The two groups set up four teams of scouts, who were trained and tested by Dr. Li Xuanguo, the person in charge of epidemic prevention work, and went to the Gaogiao Hygiene Model District in Pudong for practice on the 19th. It is now learned that the service scouts in the Baoshan District have been led by Xie Yanbo, the director of the district, and departed yesterday afternoon. The Jiading District was also led by Lu Yutian and left Shanghai at the same time. The staff working in Taicang and Kunshan will set out tomorrow.

LOCAL NEWS TWO

Small Student Robbed of Diamond Ring 183

The thief pawned the diamond ring

And then sold the pawn ticket

Tu Zhongming, a sixteen-year-old resident of No. 15, Lafei De Road, Lapei Fang, in the French Concession, attends a certain school. He goes to school alone every day, wearing a gold diamond ring worth 200 yuan on his finger. The bandit Zheng Bangyan coveted it. On the morning of the 29th of last month at 8:00 a.m., Zheng waited on the way and saw Tu carrying his schoolbag into the school. Zheng immediately stepped forward to block his way, forcibly robbed the diamond ring, and fled. He took the loot to a pawnshop and pawned it for 30 yuan, which he spent. Later, he entrusted Li Kaifang, the owner of a barbershop at No. 55, Gelo Ke Road, to introduce a pawn ticket. He got 14 yuan and sold it to Yao Laosi, a housewife at No. 45, Yin Yu Li. Now, Zhou Xianglin and Hu Fuchen, detectives of the French Concession, have found out about it and arrested all the above people and taken them to the police station. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Criminal Division 1 of the Second Special District Court. First, the police lawyer Chen Ming explained the case and stated that the first defendant was being prosecuted for armed robbery under Article 346 of the Criminal Law, and the second defendant was being prosecuted for receiving stolen goods under Article 376 of the Criminal Law. He requested that the law be applied to the trial. When Zheng Bangyan was interrogated, he confessed to blocking the road and robbing. Yao Laosi admitted to receiving stolen goods. Judge Xiong verified the confession and announced that the hearing would be adjourned to a later date. The defendants were returned to custody pending further instructions.

Xu Yabo's Residence Unsealed 184

After Xu Yabo, the former chief of the water police district, was charged with robbery and arrested, firearms and ammunition were found in his Yalu residence in Minhang, and the house was sealed. However, the Songjiang County Court had already held a hearing and sentenced Xu Yabo to seven years in prison for the robbery. As for the private possession of firearms, he was fined 200 yuan. After Xu was sentenced, he appealed the robbery conviction. He has already paid the fine for the private possession of firearms. Now, Xu's brother Xu Shengbo and Xu's wife Xu Wangshi have submitted a request to the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department to have the house returned. Woman Attempts Suicide by Jumping into River After Quarrel with Mother 186

Luckily Rescued by Patrol Boat

Cai Wenpei, a local woman, 20 years old, residing at No. 52, Fuyou Road, in the city, suddenly went to the Lan Road pier in Pudong the day before yesterday and took a ferry across the river. When the ferry reached the center of the river, the woman suddenly jumped into the river to commit suicide. Fortunately, the boatman managed to rescue her. A patrol boat from the Customs Water Patrol Police Station happened to pass by and took her to the police station. When asked about the reason for her suicide, she claimed that she had a quarrel with her mother and became disillusioned with life. The police chief, without questioning whether her statement was true, sent detective Yao Guofa to send her home and instructed her to be carefully guarded to prevent her from repeating the attempt.

Nanjing Hotel Preparing to Open 187

The Nanjing Hotel on Shanxi Road, Nanjing Road (i.e., Basin Lane) in this city has been under preparation for more than a year. The hotel has built a seven-story building, which has now been completely completed. It is towering and magnificent, and its architecture is the epitome of modern art. It was designed by the famous architect Yang Xiliu. The interior layout is particularly novel. Even the smallest details of a table and a chair are exquisitely modern and beautiful. Each guest room is equipped with a wireless telephone to break the monotony of the guest. Each bathroom is made of natural marble and has both a basin and a shower. The above points have opened up the trend of the Shanghai hotel industry. The attached Nanjing Sichuan Cuisine Restaurant is specially managed by Mr. Liao, a cooking expert from Sichuan. The Nanjing Western Cuisine Restaurant is also run by Mr. Mao and Mr. Zhu, veterans in the field, in order to satisfy the elegant tastes of Shanghai's old diners. The auditorium is entirely made of marble, magnificent and luxurious, and can be used for celebrations. General Manager Wu Ruisheng has been in the hotel industry for many years. In addition, the location was once known as the birthplace of the hotel industry center. With the advantage of location and harmony, the prosperity of the business in the future can be predicted. It is heard that the official opening will be in mid-June.

Hubei Official Cloth Sets Up Consignment Office in Shanghai 188

The Hubei Official Cloth Bureau was founded by Zhang Wenxiang dozens of years ago. Its products are most famous for the 17-pound Tianzi Official Cloth. In recent times, as a result of the economic aggression of Japanese imperialism, the sales of cloth have been completely seized. It once closed down. Recently, Han Kou merchant Wang Jingqing and others, realizing the pain of the outflow of rights and interests and the unemployment of workers, gathered huge sums of money to rent the bureau. The bureau will continue to produce the already famous Yellow Crane Tower brand yarns and 17-pound Tianzi Official Cloth, and add 16-pound to 9-pound Jiufu brand cloth to meet the needs of society and resist enemy goods for a long time. It is also heard that in order to promote business, a consignment office has been set up at No. 36, Hu Si Jing Road.

Verification of Electrician's Death from Fall 196

Qian Quanfu, a 19-year-old electrician from Liyang employed by Daoming Motor Electric Company, accidentally fell from the fifth floor of Wing On Company outside Nanjing Road, Yinghua Street, at 6:30 p.m. the day before yesterday while installing electric lights. He was seriously injured. The Lao Zha Police Station in charge received the report and ordered Detective Zhu Jiantang to investigate. After investigating, he sent him to the hospital. He died shortly after ineffective treatment. The body was moved to the Philander Road Morgue. Yesterday morning, Li Ying, a coroner appointed by the First Special District Court, arrived at the morgue and verified the body. Chen Ruikun testified that the deceased was working on an iron plate at the time, but the iron plate suddenly came off, causing him to fall to his death. Qian Aibao, the father of the deceased, testified that he was also installing electric lights at the scene, but he was too far away from his son to witness the accident. Li took the testimony and declared that the deceased, Qian Quanfu, a male, had died from injuries to his head, back, and legs sustained in the fall. The body was handed over to his father, Qian Aibao, who signed for it to be taken back for burial.

Zhabei Wang Jiazhai Ten Road Business Association Holds Meeting 200

The Zhabei Wang Jiazhai Ten Road Business Association held a meeting of the Executive Supervisory Committee yesterday. Eleven people attended. Cao Youguang presided over the meeting. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, the following motions were discussed: (1) To reorganize the remaining shops of members after the robbery. It was resolved to assign the investigation department to conduct the investigation first. (2) To persuade the shops that have not yet resumed business to resume business as soon as possible. If there are any difficulties, the association will be responsible for guaranteeing. It was resolved to pass the motion. (3) The association's expenses will be temporarily funded by the members. It was resolved to pass the motion. (4) It was resolved that the association's original location on Songyuan Road had been destroyed by artillery fire and will be temporarily attached to the Chinese Industrial School, Zi Shou Li, Qiujiang Road. It was resolved to pass the motion. (5) The chairman reported that Mr. Ye Fu Kang, a lawyer and owner of Zi Shou Li, had made appropriate arrangements for reducing and exempting rent. In addition to waiving the rent for the second, third, fourth, fifth months for old tenants, it was agreed to pay 70% of the rent from June to the end of this year. If the municipal government determines a method that is less than 70%, it should be handled in accordance with the method stipulated by the municipal government. If it is more than 70%, it should be paid at 70%. Mr. Ye has personally approved this plan. Should we thank such a wise owner? It was resolved that the owner's consideration of the times and his implementation of rent reduction is rare. The association should send a letter of thanks on behalf of the residents of the neighborhood, and forward it to the Rent Reduction Committee for filing. (6) According to the report of the tenants of Huihai Li, Qiujiang Road, the owner, Zhong Huiji, forced the tenants to increase the rent by 5 yuan per building. Those who did not agree were immediately ordered to be surrounded by bamboo fences to prevent tenants from entering and leaving. It was resolved to send a letter to the owner advising him. If he does not agree, a letter will be sent to the Transportation Committee for negotiation. (7) The Zhabei Charity Group will hold a Taoist ceremony on the 28th of this month to commemorate the martyrs of the Songhu Anti-Japanese War and the victims, and pray for a peaceful conference. The affiliated shops on all roads should be notified to prepare ingots and participate. It was resolved to pass the motion. The meeting adjourned.

Investigation of Fire at Ping An Moving Company 201

Ping An Moving Company, a double-front store at No. 752-755, at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Rue de Belles in the French Concession, caught fire a few days ago, burning to death two brothers, Sun Caisheng and Sun Fusheng, who were sleeping in the mezzanine. The details have been briefly reported in the previous newspaper. It has now been found by the police that the company has committed illegal acts. Yesterday, Gu Jianping, the owner of the company, was summoned to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer Chen Ming explained the case, stating that the defendant should not have allowed his partners to sleep on the cars or in the mezzanine built under the frame, in violation of Article 8 of the Vehicle Regulations of the Public Works Department. He requested an investigation. Gu Jianping confessed that he opened the Ping An Moving Company with a total capital of more than 10,000 yuan, and there was no insurance. He did not know how the fire started this time, which burned all the vehicles and killed two people. He requested leniency. Judge Zhang verified the confession and ordered the defendant to be released on bail pending a hearing on a later date.

Arrest and Investigation of Illegal Production of Red Pills 202

Xu Fuqing, a detective, and Zou Yunsheng and Lu Zhaolin, deputy detectives of the Joffre Police Station in the French Concession, learned that someone was privately manufacturing and selling toxic red pills in the pavilion room at No. 4, Min Shen Fang, Route Min Teh Ni, which not only violated the ban but also endangered life. Therefore, at 6:30 p.m. the day before yesterday, they led the detectives on duty to the address and arrested Yang Qingming, a native of Guangdong, who was illegally manufacturing the pills. They seized 32 pounds of red pills, 7 pounds of raw material white powder, and manufacturing equipment: an oven, a sieve, a bamboo mat, and a rattan clip. They were all taken to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the Criminal Division 1 of the Second Special Court. Fei Xizhen, a police lawyer, first explained the case and prosecuted him under Article 6 of the Opium Suppression Law, stating that the defendant was privately manufacturing and selling opium substitutes for profit and requested that he be severely punished according to law. When the defendant Yang Qingming was questioned, his confession was initially evasive and cunning. After repeated rebuttal, he confessed to the private manufacturing without hesitation. Finally, the detective in charge reported the circumstances of the capture and the search, and submitted the evidence to the court. President Wang verified the confession and ordered a further review at a later date. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Gasoline Boat Sailor Drowns 203

Yesterday morning at 3:50 a.m., the No. 14 gasoline boat of the Huangpu Steamship Company on Jiujiang Road departed from the company's wharf to the Dada Wharf in Pudong to pick up passengers. Shortly after leaving the wharf, Wang Xinhua, a sailor (31 years old, from Pudong) lost his footing and suddenly fell into the river and drowned on the spot. The body sank without a trace.

In recent days, visitors have been very crowded.

within 24 hours, the local temperature was a maximum of 82.6 and a minimum of 70.5. On the same day last year, the maximum was 92.5 and the minimum was 70.3.

Letter 233

To the esteemed editor: Having read the report in your newspaper about my injury and that of Mr. Tian in a car accident, I find it does not correspond with the facts. I am an employee of Tongcheng Company, and only sustained minor skin abrasions on both legs. Mr. Tian also only suffered external injuries. I hired a car to take him to Renji Hospital for treatment, after which he immediately left. The rumors are untrue, and I hereby make a correction. Respectfully submitted, Sheng Liangchen, Principal Writer, Local News Section, Shen Bao. June 24th.
